 isamen chunavi vigyaapan (election Advertisement) kharidne vaale vyakti or sambandhit vigyaapan kii jaankaree hogi

 google ne bayaan main kaha, " online chunavi vigyaapan main or paardarshita laane ke liye company bharat par kendrit ek 'raajnneetik vigyaapan paardarshita report' or ek saarvajanik online raajnneetik vigyaapan librari (online Political Advertisement Library) pesh karegi jise log search kar sakenge
